## Idea

A **natural isomorphism** `γ` from
[functor](category-theory.functors-precategories.md) `F : C → D` to `G : C → D`
is a
[natural transformation](category-theory.natural-transformations-functors-precategories.md)
from `F` to `G` such that the morphism `γ F : hom (F x) (G x)` is an
[isomorphism](category-theory.isomorphisms-in-precategories.md), for every
object `x` in `C`.

## Definition

### Families of isomorphisms between functors

### The identity natural isomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8814" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8821" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8821" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="8825" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8826" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8826" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="8830" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8830" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="8834" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8834" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="8838" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8838" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="8842" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8844" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="8849" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="8922" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8922" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="8958" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="8964" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8965" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8965" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="8968" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8970" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3980" class="Function">functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="8991" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8854" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="8994" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8884" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a><a id="8996" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8998" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9000" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4900" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9033" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8854" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9036" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8884" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9039" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8965" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9042" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8965" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a>
  <a id="9047" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8922" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9083" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9083" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9086" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="9092" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8718" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-map-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9132" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8854" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9135" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8884" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a>
      <a id="9144" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9146" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4760" class="Function">map-functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9171" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8854" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9174" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8884" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9177" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9083" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="9179" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Equalities induce natural isomorphisms

An equality between functors `F` and `G` gives rise to a natural isomorphism
between them. This is because, by the J-rule, it is enough to construct a
natural isomorphism given `refl : F ＝ F`, from `F` to itself. We take the
identity natural transformation as such an isomorphism.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="natural-isomorphism-eq-Precategoryᵉ"></a><a id="9520" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9520" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-eq-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9556" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="9560" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9561" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9561" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="9565" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9565" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="9569" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9569" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="9573" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9573" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="9577" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9579" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9584" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="9588" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9589" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9589" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9592" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9594" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9607" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9561" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="9611" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9565" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="9614" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9619" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9619" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9622" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9624" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9637" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9569" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="9641" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9573" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a><a id="9644" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="9648" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9649" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9649" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9652" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9652" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="9655" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9657" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3980" class="Function">functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9678" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9589" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9681" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9619" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a><a id="9683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9685" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="9689" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9649" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9692" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="9695" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9652" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="9698" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9700" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4900" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9733" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9589" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9736" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9619" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9739" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9649" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="9742" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9652" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a>

  <a id="9804" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8922" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="9840" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9781" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="9843" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9784" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="9846" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9787" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a>

## Propositions

### Being a natural isomorphism is a proposition

That a natural transformation is a natural isomorphism is a proposition. This
follows from the fact that being an isomorphism is a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="10074" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10081" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10081" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="10085" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10086" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10086" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="10090" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10090" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="10094" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10094" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="10098" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10098" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="10102" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10104" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="10109" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Equality of natural isomorphisms is equality of their underlying natural transformations

<pre class="Agda"><a id="11016" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="11023" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11023" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="11027" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11028" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11028" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="11032" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11032" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="11036" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11036" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="11040" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11040" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="11044" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11046" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="11051" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="11055" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11056" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="11059" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11061" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="11074" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11028" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="11078" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11032" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="11081" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11085" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11086" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="11089" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11091" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="11104" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11036" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="11108" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11040" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a><a id="11111" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11154" class="Keyword">where</a>

      <a id="11840" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5329" class="Function">natural-transformation-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="11896" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="11899" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="11902" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11116" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="11905" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11119" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="11908" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11701" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="11910" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11912" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="11918" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11698" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="11921" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="11924" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11701" class="Bound">gᵉ</a>
  <a id="11929" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11629" class="Function">eq-eq-natural-transformation-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="11991" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11991" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="11994" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11994" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="11997" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="12003" href="foundation-core.subtypes%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4286" class="Function">eq-type-subtypeᵉ</a> <a id="12020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12021" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#10589" class="Function">is-natural-isomorphism-prop-hom-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12066" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12069" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12072" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11116" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12075" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11119" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="12077" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="12144" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12145" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12145" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="12148" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12148" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="12151" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12153" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4900" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12186" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12189" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12192" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11116" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12195" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11119" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="12197" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12199" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="12205" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12207" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5674" class="Function">hom-family-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12251" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12254" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12257" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11116" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12260" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11119" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="12263" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12145" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="12266" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2800" class="Function Operator">~ᵉ</a>
      <a id="12275" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5674" class="Function">hom-family-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12319" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12322" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12325" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11116" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="12328" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11119" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="12331" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12148" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="12333" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12335" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="12341" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12145" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="12344" href="foundation-core.identity-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2730" class="Function Operator">＝ᵉ</a> <a id="12347" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12148" class="Bound">gᵉ</a>
  <a id="12352" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12082" class="Function">eq-htpy-hom-family-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12404" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="12410" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-maps-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12343" class="Function">eq-htpy-hom-family-natural-isomorphism-map-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12466" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12469" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a>
      <a id="12478" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12480" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4760" class="Function">map-functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12505" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12508" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12511" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11116" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="12513" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="12521" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12523" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4760" class="Function">map-functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12548" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11056" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12551" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11086" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="12554" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#11119" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="12556" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The type of natural isomorphisms form a set

The type of natural isomorphisms between functors `F` and `G` is a
[subtype](foundation-core.subtypes.md) of the [set](foundation-core.sets.md)
`natural-transformation F G` since being an isomorphism is a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="12839" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="12846" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12846" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="12850" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12851" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12851" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="12855" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12855" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="12859" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12859" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="12863" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12863" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="12867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12869" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="12874" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="12878" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12879" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12879" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="12882" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12884" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="12897" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12851" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="12901" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#12855" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="12904" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="23454" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23456" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4760" class="Function">map-functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="23481" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22574" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="23484" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22604" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="23487" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22634" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a><a id="23489" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23497" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23499" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4760" class="Function">map-functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="23524" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22574" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="23527" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22604" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="23530" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22637" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="23532" class="Symbol">)</a>

#### Composition of natural isomorphisms satisfies inverse laws

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24661" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24668" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24668" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="24672" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24673" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24673" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="24677" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24677" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="24681" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24681" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="24685" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24685" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="24689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24691" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="24696" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="24700" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24701" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24701" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="24704" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24706" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="24719" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24673" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="24723" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24677" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="24726" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24799" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24800" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24800" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="24803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24805" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4900" class="Function">natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="24838" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24701" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="24841" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24731" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="24844" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24761" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="24847" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24764" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="24849" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24853" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24862" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24862" class="Function">left-inverse-law-comp-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="24917" class="Symbol">:</a>

    <a id="25534" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25536" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8922" class="Function">id-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="25572" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24701" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="25575" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24731" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="25578" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24764" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="25580" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="25761" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25763" href="category-theory.functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#4760" class="Function">map-functor-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="25788" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24701" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="25791" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24731" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="25794" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24764" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="25796" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="25804" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25806" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24800" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="25808" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### When the type of natural transformations is a proposition, the type of natural isomorphisms is a proposition

The type of natural isomorphisms between functors `F` and `G` is a subtype of
`natural-transformation F G`, so when this type is a proposition, then the type
of natural isomorphisms from `F` to `G` form a proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="26156" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="26163" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26163" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="26167" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26168" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26168" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="26172" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26172" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="26176" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26176" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="26180" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26180" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="26184" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26186" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="26191" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="26195" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26196" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26196" class="Bound">Cᵉ</a> <a id="26199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26201" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="26214" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26168" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="26218" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26172" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a><a id="26221" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="26225" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26226" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26226" class="Bound">Dᵉ</a> <a id="26229" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26231" href="category-theory.precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3370" class="Function">Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="26244" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26176" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="26248" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26180" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a><a id="26251" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="26294" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="26303" href="category-theory.natural-isomorphisms-functors-precategories%25E1%25B5%2589.html#26303" class="Function">is-prop-natural-isomorphism-Precategoryᵉ</a> <a id="26344" class="Symbol">:</a>
